('Robert P.', '5.0 out of 5 stars', "\nSo, being someone who loves the challenge of confirming, or disproving outlandish claims from manufactures, I was keen to test the claim by Thermos of keeping things hot or cold for 24 hours.  Having had numerous flasks in the past, which on a good day would do the job for 6 hours or so, the challenge was on.  So after filling with hot, not boiling water I took the temperature of the contents, and found it to be 59 degC.  24 hours later, it had dropped to 47 degC.  I can only speak for myself here, but, I was more than impressed.  The flask itself seems robust, and should survive a certain amount of mistreatment, that's not to say it's indestructible, as anyone with children will know, even Tonka toys are no match for a determined 4 year old, or a 9 kg load washing machine no match for a determined wife, but that's another story.  The poring system is of the quarter to half a turn then pour variety, rather than some of the more elaborate systems, which seem to fail after a while.  This is simple, and relies on a single silicone rubber seal.  It also give a predictable flow from the spout, and no drips running down the side of the flask.  So well done Thermos, your claims are justified, you have made an excellent product.  I would not hesitate in recommending this to friends, and may well now look at getting one of their food flasks as well.\n")
